Section 8. Tax Covenants.
(a) The City covenants that:
(i) it will use, and will restrict the
use and investment of, the proceeds of
the Series 2016 Bonds in such manner
and to such extent as may be necessary so that (a) the interest on the
Series 2016 Bonds will be excluded
from gross income for federal income
tax purposes, and (b) in the case of
any Series 2016 Bonds qualifying as
bonds, the interest on which is not
treated as an item of tax preference
under Section 57 of the Code
(“Non–AMT Bonds”), such Series 2016
Bonds will be treated as Non–AMT
Bonds.
(ii) (A) it will take or cause to be
taken such actions that may be
required of it for the interest on the
Series 2016 Bonds to be and to remain
excluded from gross income for federal income tax purposes, (B) it will not
take or authorize to be taken any
actions that would adversely affect
that exclusion, and (C) it, or persons
acting for it, will, among other acts of
compliance, (1) apply the proceeds of
the Series 2016 Bonds to the governmental purposes of the borrowing, (2)
restrict the yield on investment property, (3) make timely and adequate
payments to the federal government,
(4) maintain books and records and
make calculations and reports, and
(5) refrain from certain uses of those
proceeds and, as applicable, of property financed with such proceeds, all in
such manner and to the extent necessary to assure such exclusion of that
interest under the Code.
(b) Further Actions. The Director
of Finance, or any other officer of the
City
having
responsibility
for
issuance of the Series 2016 Bonds, is

Section 12. Financial Advisors and
Consultants.
The Director of Finance may obtain
the services of one or more Financial
Advisors, from time to time, to assist
the Director of Finance in making
any of the determinations required by
this Series 2016 Bond Ordinance to be
made by the Director of Finance with
respect to the Series 2016 Bonds and
any Credit Support Instruments. The
Director of Finance may rely on the
written advice of any Financial Advisor so retained. The Director of Public
Utilities may obtain the services of
one or more feasibility consultants,
from time to time, to provide reports
in connection with the issuance and
sale of any Series 2016 Bonds concerning the utilization and operation of
the System, debt service coverage,
rates and charges or other matters.
Any Financial Advisor or consultant
employed under the authority of this
Series 2016 Bond Ordinance shall be
disinterested in the transaction and
be independent of the Original Purchasers or any other party interested
in the transaction.
Section 13. Appointment of Trustee.
The Director of Finance is hereby
authorized to appoint an initial
Trustee in the Certificate of Award
and to appoint a successor Trustee in
the event that the initial Trustee
shall resign or be removed or dissolved or otherwise become incapable
of acting as Trustee under the Trust
Agreement, or in case it shall be
taken under the control of any public
officer or officers or of a receiver
appointed by a court, in accordance
with the provisions of the Master
Trust Agreement.
Section 14. Authorization and
Requirement of Declarations of Official Intent.
The Director of Finance, in consultation with the Director of Public Utilities, is authorized to prepare and
sign declarations of official intent in
the form required by United States
Treasury Regulations §1.150-2 (the
“Reimbursement Regulations”) with
respect to original expenditures to
which the Reimbursement Regulations apply, to be made from money
temporarily advanced for improvements to the System and that is reasonably expected to be reimbursed
from the proceeds of the Series 2016
Bonds or other obligations; to make
appropriate reimbursement and timely allocations from the proceeds of the
Series 2016 Bonds or other obligations
to reimburse such original expenditures; and to take any other actions as
may be appropriate, all at the times
and in the manner required under the
Reimbursement Regulations in order
for the reimbursement to be treated
as an expenditure of such proceeds
for purposes of Sections 103 and 141 to
150 of the Code. No advance from any
fund or account or order for payment
may be made for original expenditures
(other
than
expenditures

152

February 3, 2016
excepted from such requirement
under the Reimbursement Regulations) that are to be reimbursed subsequently from proceeds of Series
2016 Bonds or other obligations,
unless a declaration of official intent
with respect thereto is made within
the time required by the Reimbursement Regulations.
Section 15. Open Meeting Determination.
It is found and determined that all
formal actions of the Council concerning and relating to the adoption of
this Series 2016 Bond Ordinance were
adopted in an open meeting of the
Council, and that all deliberations of
the Council and of any of its committees that resulted in such formal
action were in meetings open to the
public in compliance with all applicable legal requirements.
Section 16. Separability.
Each section of this Series 2016
Bond Ordinance and each subdivision
of any section is declared to be independent, and the finding or holding of
any section or subdivision of any section to be invalid or void shall not be
deemed or held to affect the validity
of any other section or subdivision of
this Series 2016 Bond Ordinance.
Section 17. Recitals.
It is determined and recited that all
acts, conditions and things necessary
to be done precedent to and in the
issuing of the Series 2016 Bonds in
order to make them legal, valid and
binding special obligations of the
City will have happened, been done
and performed or will happen, be done
and performed in regular and due
form as required by law; and that no
limitation of indebtedness or taxation, either statutory or constitutional, is applicable to the issuance of the
Series 2016 Bonds.
Section 18. Sunset of Authorization.
The authority granted by Section 2
of this Series 2016 Bond Ordinance to
issue Series 2016 Bonds shall expire
three years from the effective date of
this Series 2016 Bond Ordinance. If a
preliminary official statement with
respect to the issuance of Series 2016
Bonds is distributed under the authority of this Series 2016 Bond Ordinance
at any time within the three-year period following its effective date, then
the authority granted by this Series
2016 Bond Ordinance shall not expire
as to the Series 2016 Bonds. The Director of Finance shall notify the Chairman of the Finance Committee and
the Clerk of this Council of the initiation of the issuance of Series 2016
Bonds under the authority of this
Series 2016 Bond Ordinance.
Section 19. Emergency.
This Series 2016 Bond Ordinance is
declared to be an emergency measure
and, provided it receives the affirmative vote of two-thirds of all the members elected to Council, it shall take
effect and be in force immediately
upon its adoption and approval by the
Mayor; otherwise, it shall take effect
and be in force from and after the earliest period allowed by law.
Passed January 25, 2016.
Effective January 26, 2016.

An emergency ordinance authorizing the issuance and sale of Water
Pollution Control Revenue Bonds of
the city for the purpose of paying

February 3, 2016
costs of improvements to the Water
Pollution Control system; authorizing
a master trust agreement to secure
Water Pollution Control Revenue
Bonds of the city; authorizing and
related
matters;
and
approving
declaring an emergency.
Whereas, pursuant to Article XVIII
of the Constitution of the State of
Ohio (the “State”) and the Charter of
the City of Cleveland, Ohio, the City of
Cleveland, Ohio (the “City”), a municipal corporation and political subdivision in and of the State, is authorized
(a) to own and operate, and does own
and operate, as a public utility a
wastewater collection and disposal
system (as defined in more detail
herein, the “System”), (b) to make,
from time to time, additions, extensions or improvements to the System,
(c) to issue bonds and notes and
refunding bonds and notes for any
such purpose or purposes, and (d) to
secure any bonds or notes so issued by
a pledge of and lien on the net revenues of the System; and
Whereas, the Council of the City of
Cleveland hereby determines the
necessity and intention of the City to
improve the System by making additions, extensions and improvements
to the System to provide users of the
System with continued service, and
further determines that the issue, sale
and delivery of revenue bonds is
required to finance the costs of such
additions, extensions and improvements,
together
with
funding
reserves and paying expenses incidental to such financings; and
Whereas, the Council of the City of
Cleveland hereby determines to
authorize the issuance of such revenue bonds, which revenue bonds
shall be equally and ratably payable
from and secured by a pledge of and
lien on the net revenues of the System; and
Whereas, pursuant to Ordinance No.
28-16, passed by the Council of the
City of Cleveland on the same date as
the date of its adoption of this General Bond Ordinance, the Council of the
City of Cleveland has authorized the
issuance of a series of such revenue
bonds to be designated “Water Pollution Control Revenue Bonds, Series
2016” (the “Series 2016 Bonds” and,
together with such additional bonds
as may be authorized, from time to
time, on a parity therewith, “Bonds”)
for the purpose of making additions,
extensions or improvements to the
System; and
Whereas, the Council of the City of
Cleveland has further determined
that it is necessary for the City to
enter into a trust agreement to secure
the Bonds by a pledge of and lien on
the net revenues of the System and
other pledged funds, all as set forth
and declared in this General Bond
Ordinance, and otherwise to provide
for the security thereof;
Now, therefore, be it ordained by
the Council of the City of Cleveland
that:
Section 1. Definitions. The following words and terms, as used in this
General Bond Ordinance, in the Trust
Agreement, as hereinafter defined,
and in the Bonds, as hereinafter
defined, shall have the following
meanings unless otherwise expressly
provided therein or unless the context
indicates another meaning or intent:
“Additional Bonds” means the Additional Bonds authorized to be issued
pursuant to Section 5 hereof, irrespective of whether such Additional

The City Record
Bonds are designated bonds or notes.
“Adjusted Net Revenues” means, for
any period, Net Revenues Available
for Debt Service adjusted to reflect
increases or decreases resulting from
the following:
(a) Rates in effect at the time of
issuance of the proposed Series of
Additional Bonds;
(b) Revenues anticipated to be generated based upon rates established
(and to be placed in effect within two
(2) years from the date of issuance of
the proposed Series of Additional
Bonds) in a rate ordinance adopted by
the Council prior to the issuance of
the proposed Series of Additional
Bonds;
(c) Additional Net Revenues anticipated to result from any addition,
extension or improvement to the System that the City has constructed and
that is in operation on the date of
issuance of the proposed Series of
Additional Bonds, but that was not in
operation during the entire period;
(d) Additional Net Revenues anticipated to result from the operation of
existing facilities or existing collection systems that the City will
acquire or commence operating with
the proceeds of the proposed Series of
Additional Bonds; and
(e) Changes in Operating Expenses
anticipated to result from any additions, extensions and improvements
to the System to be financed with the
proposed Series of Additional Bonds.
“Appreciated Principal Amount”
means, as of any date of computation
with respect to any Capital Appreciation Bond, an amount equal to the
principal amount thereof at its initial
offering plus an amount of interest
that, based on semiannual compounding on each Compounding Date from
the date of delivery on the basis of a
360-day year of twelve 30-day months,
will produce a yield approximately
equal to the yield to maturity for such
Bond specified in or pursuant to the
applicable Supplemental Bond Ordinance. A schedule setting forth the
Appreciated Principal Amount of
Capital Appreciation Bonds as of the
Compounding Dates may be set forth
in the form of such Capital Appreciation Bond. The Appreciated Principal
Amount with respect to any date
other than the Compounding Dates is
the Appreciated Principal Amount on
the next preceding Compounding
Date or dated date as noted on the
form thereof, as the case may be, plus
the fraction of the difference between
the Appreciated Principal Amount on
such next preceding Compounding
Date or dated date and the next succeeding Compounding Date that
equals the ratio of (a) the number of
days from such next preceding Compounding Date or dated date to the
date for which the determination is
being calculated to (b) the total number of days from such next preceding
Compounding Date or dated date to
the next succeeding Compounding
Date.
“Assumed Amortization Period”
means the period of time specified in
paragraph (a) or paragraph (b)
below, as selected by the Director of
Finance:
(a) Five (5) years; or
(b) The period of time, exceeding
five (5) years, set forth in a written
opinion delivered to the City, of a
Financial Expert, as being not longer
than the maximum period of time
over which indebtedness having comparable terms and security issued or

Obligations that on deposit in a

definition of “Crossover Refunded
Bonds.”

with respect to any particular
Crossover Refunding Bonds and
Crossover Refunded Bonds, the date
on which the Crossover Amount on
deposit in a Crossover Escrow Fund
shall be used to retire all such Outstanding Crossover Refunded Bonds

Fund was established.
“Crossover Escrow Fund” means an
escrow account in which a Crossover
Amount is deposited.
“Crossover Escrow Deposit Agreement” means an escrow deposit agreement under which a Crossover
Escrow Fund is created and administered.
“Crossover Refunded Bond” means
any Bond deemed to be Crossover
Refunded. Any one or more of the
Bonds shall be deemed to have been
Crossover Refunded and shall be
deemed to be Crossover Refunded
Bonds if:
(a) The Trustee shall have received
and shall hold in trust for and irrevocably committed thereto, moneys sufficient, or
(b) The Trustee shall have received
and shall hold in trust for and irrevocably committed thereto, Defeasance
Obligations that are certified by an
independent certified public accountant to be of such maturities, irrevocably established redemption dates or
irrevocably established repurchase
dates (if such Defeasance Obligations are subject to a repurchase
agreement) and interest payment
dates, and to be of such principal
amounts or irrevocably established
redemption prices and to bear such
interest, which together with any
moneys to which reference is made in
paragraph (a) above, without the
need for further investment or reinvestment of either the principal
amount thereof or the interest earnings therefrom (which earnings are
to be held likewise in trust, except as
provided herein), will be sufficient:
(i) for the payment of all principal
of and premium, if any, on such
Crossover Refunded Bonds as the
same become due, whether at their
maturity or redemption dates or otherwise, as the case may be, or if a
default in payment shall have
occurred on any maturity or redemption date, then for the payment of all
principal of and premium on such
Crossover Refunded Bonds to the date
of the tender of payment; provided,
that if any of those Crossover Refunded Bonds are to be redeemed prior to
the maturity thereof, notice of that
redemption shall have been duly
given or irrevocable provision shall
have been duly made for the giving of
that notice, and
(ii) for the payment of interest (in
whole or in part) on any Crossover
Refunding Bonds, the proceeds of
which were, in whole or in part,
deposited in such Crossover Escrow
Fund, or both. Prior to the Crossover
Date, the Crossover Amount may be
pledged as security for the Crossover
Refunding Bonds, the Crossover
Refunded Bonds, or both. The moneys

“Debt Service” for any period
means, except as otherwise provided
herein, as of any date of calculation
with respect to any Series, an amount
equal to the sum of (i) interest due
during such period on the Bonds of
such Series, (ii) the principal amount,
as of the beginning of such period, of
Outstanding Bonds of such Series that
mature on any future date in such
period, reduced by the aggregate
principal amount of such Bonds that
would at or before that future date
cease to be Outstanding by reason,
but only by reason, of the application
of Sinking Fund Installments at or
before that future date, and (iii) the
amount of any Sinking Fund Installment with respect to the Bonds of
such Series required to be paid on any
future date in such period (calculated
on the assumption that Bonds Outstanding at the date of calculation
will not cease to be Outstanding
except by reason of payment on the
due date thereof or redemption from
Sinking Fund Installments); provided
that for purposes of computing the
Additional Bonds test in Section
5(h)(iii) hereof, the rate covenant
contained in Section 20(c) hereof, and
any Debt Service Reserve Requirement hereunder, the interest component of Debt Service with respect to a
Series of Bonds shall be reduced by
any accrued interest or capitalized
interest funded from the proceeds of
Bonds, and, for the first annual period
following the issuance of such Series
of Bonds, shall not include more than
one year’s interest.

“Interest Rate Hedge Agreement”
means an interest rate swap, an interest rate cap or other such arrangement obtained by the City, in accordance with applicable law in effect at
the time, with the goal of (i) lowering
the effective interest rate to the City
on Bonds, (ii) hedging the exposure
of the City with respect to its obligations on Bonds against fluctuations in
prevailing interest rates; (iii) otherwise reducing risk (including, without limitation, in addition to interest
rate risk, tax risk or liquidity renewal risk) or otherwise managing exposure to changing markets (including,
without limitation, in advance of
issuances of Bonds); (iv) achieving a
more appropriate matching of its
assets and liabilities; and (v) otherwise pursuing an optimal capital
structure.

Section 2. Master Trust Agreement.
To provide for the issuance of and
security for the Series 2016 Bonds and
subsequent Series of Additional
Bonds, the Mayor and the Director of
Finance are authorized and directed,
for and in the name and on behalf of
the City, to execute, acknowledge and
deliver the Master Trust Agreement,
approved as to form and correctness
by the Director of Law, not inconsistent with this General Bond Ordinance and not substantially adverse
to the City, as may be approved by the
officers signing the same on behalf of
the City. The determination by those
officers that the Master Trust Agreement is not substantially adverse to
the City shall be conclusively evidenced by the signing and delivery of
the Master Trust Agreement by those
officers. The Mayor, the Director of
Finance, the Director of Public Utilities and the Director of Law, as appropriate, are further authorized and
directed to execute any Certifications, financing statements, assignments, and instruments that they
deem necessary or appropriate to perfect the assignments set forth in the
Master Trust Agreement and to consummate the transactions contemplated by the Master Trust Agreement.
Section 3. Terms of Bonds; Pledge
of and Lien on Net Revenues.
(a) The Bonds of each Series shall
be designated “Water Pollution Control Revenue Bonds” and contain an
appropriate Series designation. The
Bonds of each Series shall be payable
as to principal, redemption premium,
if any, and interest, unless otherwise
provided in or pursuant to the Supplemental Bond Ordinance with respect
to a Series of Bonds, in lawful money
of the United States of America, shall
be in fully registered form (unless a
Supplemental Trust Agreement shall
have been executed and delivered
pursuant to Section 7.01(b)(vi) of the
Master Trust Agreement), shall be
negotiable instruments in accordance
with the Ohio Revised Code, and shall
expressly set forth the purpose or purposes for which the Series of Bonds is
issued and such other statements or
legends as may be required by law. As
applied to any Bond that is a Capital
Appreciation Bond, any provision of
the Trust Agreement specifying the
permitted denomination of such Bond
shall refer to the Appreciated Principal Amount thereof at its stated maturity.
(b) Unless otherwise provided in
the applicable Supplemental Bond
Ordinance or Supplemental Trust
Agreement, the Bonds of each Series
shall originally be issued solely in
Book-Entry Form to a Depository to
be held in a Book-Entry System and:
(i) the Bonds shall be registered in
the name of the Depository or its nominee, as Bondholder, and immobilized
in the custody of the Depository; (ii)
there shall, unless otherwise requested by the Depository, be a single Bond
representing each interest rate for
each maturity and Sinking Fund
Installment of the Bonds; and (iii) the
Bonds shall not be transferable or
exchangeable, except for transfer to
another Depository or another nominee of a Depository, without further
action by the City as set forth in the
next succeeding paragraph of this
Section.
If any Depository determines not to
continue to act as a Depository for the
Bonds held in a Book-Entry System,

The City Record
the City may attempt to have established a securities depository/book
entry system relationship with another Depository hereunder. If the City
does not or is unable to do so, the City
and the Trustee, after the Trustee has
made provision for notification of the
owners of book entry interests by
appropriate notice to the then Depository, shall permit withdrawal of the
Bonds from the Depository and shall
authenticate and deliver Bond certificates in fully registered form to the
assignees of the Depository or its
nominee. If the event is not the result
of City action or inaction, such withdrawal, authentication and delivery
shall be at the cost and expense
(including costs of printing or otherwise preparing, and delivering, such
replacement Bonds), of those persons
requesting such authentication and
delivery.
(c) Unless otherwise provided in
the applicable Supplemental Bond
Ordinance or Supplemental Trust
Agreement, the Bonds of each Series
shall be executed by the Mayor and
Director of Finance and approved as
to form by the Director of Law, each
of which signatures may be facsimiles. If any officer whose signature or
a facsimile thereof shall appear on
any Bonds shall cease to be such officer prior to the issuance, authentication or delivery of such Bonds, such
signature or such facsimile shall nevertheless be valid and sufficient for
all purposes, the same as if such officer had remained in office until that
time. The Bonds of each Series shall
bear the corporate seal of the City or a
facsimile thereof.
(d) Unless otherwise provided in
any Supplemental Bond Ordinance,
notice of the call for redemption of
any of the Bonds, which notice (i)
shall specify the complete official
name of the Bonds to be redeemed,
including Series, CUSIP numbers (if
applicable), bond certificate numbers, the redemption date, the redemption price, and the place or places
where amounts due upon such
redemption will be payable (which
shall be the designated corporate
trust office of the Trustee or any Paying Agent) and, if less than all of the
Bonds are to be redeemed, the numbers of the Bonds and the portions of
Bonds, so to be redeemed, (ii) shall
state any condition to such redemption, (iii) shall state that on the
redemption date, and upon the satisfaction of any such condition, the
Bonds or portions thereof to be
redeemed shall cease to bear interest,
and (iv) may set forth any additional
information relating to such redemption, shall be given at least thirty (30)
days but not more than sixty (60)
days prior to the date fixed for
redemption by mailing a copy of the
redemption notice by first class mail
to the Holder of each Bond to be
redeemed in whole or in part at the
Holder’s address shown on the Register on the fifteenth (15th) day preceding that mailing; provided, however,
that failure to give such notice by
mailing or any defect in such notice
with respect to any Bond shall not
affect the validity of any redemption
proceedings with respect to any other
Bond.

redemption premium on any Bond and
the Appreciated Principal Amount of
any Capital Appreciation Bond shall
be payable when due, without deduction for services of the Paying Agent,

the Bonds then due, then such Person
upon such payment shall become the
owner of the principal or Appreciated
Principal Amount of and any redemption premium or interest on the Bonds
contemplated to be acquired by such
payment notwithstanding any other
provision of the Trust Agreement.
The Trustee shall pay any money
received by it from such Person to the
Holders as if it were the payment of
the principal or Appreciated Principal Amount of and any redemption
premium or interest on the Bonds
then due, and the Trustee or the Holder, whichever shall first receive such
payment, shall deliver to such Person
(i) in the case of interest on the
Bonds, an acknowledgement of such
Person’s ownership of interest to be
paid on the Bonds specifying the
amount of interest owned, the period
represented by such interest and the
numbers of the Bonds on which such
interest is owed, and (ii) in the case
of principal or Appreciated Principal
Amount of or premium on the Bonds,
either the Bonds themselves assigned
to such Person or new Bonds in
exchange for the Predecessor Bonds
naming such Person as the Holder.
Whenever moneys become available
for the payment of Defaulted Interest,
the Person to whom an acknowledgement as above has been delivered
shall be treated as to the Defaulted
Interest that is the subject of the
acknowledgement as if such Person
had been the Holder of the Bonds on
which such Defaulted Interest is
payable on the Special Record Date.
(g) Subject to the foregoing, each
Bond delivered under the Trust
Agreement upon transfer thereof, or
in exchange for or in replacement of
any other Bond, shall carry the rights
to interest accrued and unpaid, and to
accrue on that Bond, or that were carried by that Bond. Except as provided
in this Section 3 and in Section 5 hereof, (i) the Holder of any Bond shall be
deemed and regarded as the absolute
owner thereof for all purposes of the
Trust Agreement, (ii) payment of or
on account of the principal of or any
redemption premium or interest on
any Bond shall be made only to or
upon the order of that Holder or its
duly authorized attorney in the manner permitted by the Trust Agreement, and (iii) neither the City, the
Trustee, the Bond Registrar nor any
Paying Agent shall, to the extent permitted by law, be affected by notice to
the contrary. All of those payments
shall be valid and effective to satisfy
and discharge the liability upon that
Bond, including without limitation,
the interest thereon, to the extent of
the amount or amounts so paid.
(h) The Bonds shall be payable
solely from Net Revenues and, to the
extent provided herein and in the
Master Trust Agreement or any Supplemental Trust Agreement, the moneys and securities in the Special
Funds, and shall be secured only by
the Trust Agreement and by a pledge
of and lien on Net Revenues and on
the Funds and Subfunds (to the
extent the moneys and securities

160

February 3, 2016
therein constitute Net Revenues) and
on the Special Funds, subject, however, to the provisions of the Trust
Agreement providing for the application of Net Revenues and of the moneys and securities on deposit in the
various Funds and Subfunds. Neither
the State nor the City or its Council
shall be obligated to pay the principal
of or interest on the Bonds from any
other moneys or source, nor shall the
Bonds be a claim upon or lien against
any property of or under the control of
the City or the Council except Net
Revenues and the moneys and securities on deposit in the Special Funds.
The Bonds shall be secured equally
and ratably under the Trust Agreement without the priority of any Bond
over any other Bond (subject, however, to the provisions of the Trust
Agreement, including, without limitation, the provisions of Section 5(d) of
this General Bond Ordinance regarding
the
applicability
of
credit
enhancement or liquidity support to a
particular Series of Bonds). The
pledge of and lien on Net Revenues
and the moneys and securities on
deposit in the Special Funds, as created hereby, shall from the date hereof
be valid and binding. The Net Revenues and the moneys and securities
on deposit in the Special Funds so
pledged and hereafter received shall
immediately be subject to the lien of
such pledge without any physical
delivery thereof or further act, and
such lien shall be valid and binding
against all parties having claims of
any kind in tort, contract or otherwise
against the City, irrespective of
whether such parties have notice
thereof. The Bonds do not constitute a
debt or a pledge of the faith and credit of the City or of the State or of any
political subdivision thereof, and the
Holders thereof shall have no right to
have taxes levied by the Council or by
the General Assembly of the State or
taxing authority of any political subdivision of the State for the payment
of the principal thereof or the interest
thereon. The pledge of Net Revenues
and the moneys and securities on
deposit in the Special Funds shall be
effective and the moneys therefrom
may be applied to the purposes for
which pledged, as contemplated herein, without necessity of any further
act of appropriation. Nothing in this
General Bond Ordinance shall be construed as pledging the general credit
of the City or that of the State or of
any political subdivision thereof to
the payment of the Bonds or any part
thereof or interest thereon.
Section 4. Replacement of Mutilated, Lost, Stolen or Destroyed Bonds.
In case any Bond is mutilated, lost,
stolen, or destroyed, the City shall
execute and deliver a Bond of like
authority and principal amount as the
Bond so mutilated, lost, stolen, or
destroyed, in exchange and substitution for such Bond in the manner provided in the Trust Agreement.
Section 5. Authorization of the
Issuance of Bonds.
(a) Authorization. The issuance
from time to time of Bonds is hereby
authorized without limitation as to
amount except as herein provided or
as may be limited by law and in one or
more Series as hereinafter provided,
for the purpose only of paying Capital
Costs,
or
refunding,
including
advance refunding, for any lawful
purpose, any Outstanding Bonds or
Subordinated Indebtedness where
such refunding will not adversely

February 3, 2016
affect the exclusion of the interest on
any Tax-Exempt Bonds from gross
income for purposes of federal income
taxation. The issuance of each Series
of Bonds shall be authorized by a Supplemental Bond Ordinance, which
may specify, or provide for the related
Certificate of Award or Supplemental
Trust Agreement to specify, (i) the
authorized principal amount and
Series designation of the Bonds, (ii)
the purpose for which such Series is
being issued; (iii) the date, and the
maturity date or dates, of the Bonds of
such Series; (iv) the interest rate or
rates of the Bonds of such Series, or
the manner of determining such rate
or rates, and the Interest Payment
Dates therefor, and, in the case of
Variable Rate Bonds, the maximum
rate of interest payable thereon, if
any; (v) the denominations of, and the
manner of dating, numbering and lettering, the Bonds of such Series; (vi)
the Paying Agent and the place or
places of payment of the Bonds of
such Series or the manner of appointing and designating the same; (vii)
the redemption prices, if any, and the
redemption terms for the Bonds of
such Series; (viii) the amount and due
date of each Sinking Fund Installment, if any, for Term Bonds of such
Series, provided that the due date of
any Sinking Fund Installment shall
be an Interest Payment Date; (ix) the
amount of the Debt Service Reserve
Requirement, if any, with respect to
the Bonds of such Series; (x) provisions for the sale of the Bonds of such
Series; (xi) the forms of the Bonds of
such Series; and (xii) any other provisions deemed advisable by the City as
shall not conflict with the provisions
hereof and the of the Trust Agreement. A Supplemental Bond Ordinance may also authorize and provide
for the City to enter into one or more
Interest Rate Hedge Agreements
with respect to any Bonds that are
Outstanding or authorized to be
issued, and may do so prior to, simultaneously with, or subsequent to the
issuance of such Bonds. Additional
Bonds shall be equally and ratably
payable from Net Revenues and shall
be secured by a pledge of and lien on
Net Revenues and the Special Funds
on a parity with any other then Outstanding Bonds, subject, however, to
the provisions of the Trust Agreement providing for the application
thereof.
(b) Variable Rate Bonds. Any
Series of Bonds may be issued as Variable Rate Bonds. The Supplemental
Bond Ordinance and Supplemental
Trust Agreement applicable to any
Series of Variable Rate Bonds shall
specify the method and procedure by
which the rate of interest to be borne
thereby shall be determined, may provide for the right of the holders thereof to tender such Variable Rate Bonds
for purchase by the City at the times,
on the terms, and subject to the conditions set forth therein and may provide for more frequent deposits by the
City to the Debt Service Fund for
Bond Service Charges, in the event
that
payment
of
Bond
Service
Charges on such Variable Rate Bonds
is due more frequently than semiannually, but if deposits to the Debt Service Fund for Bond Service Charges
on any Series of Additional Bonds are
required to be made more frequently
than had been required for Bond Service Charges on any Outstanding
Bonds, then, from and after the
issuance of such Additional Bonds,

The City Record
deposits to the Debt Service Fund
shall be required for all Outstanding
Bonds with the same frequency as
they are required for such Additional
Bonds.
(c) Capital Appreciation Bonds. All
or any portion of any Series of Additional Bonds may be issued as Capital
Appreciation Bonds.
(d) Credit Enhancement. In addition to the Net Revenues and the Special Funds and other amounts, proceeds, moneys, investments, rights,
and interests pledged and assigned
by the City to the Trustee under the
Trust Agreement to secure the payment of the Bond Service Charges, the
Supplemental Trust Agreement for
any Series of Bonds may provide for
credit enhancement or liquidity support applicable to such Series of
Bonds without any requirement that
the security or protection afforded by
such credit enhancement or liquidity
support extend or apply to the Bonds
of any other Series. The fees, charges,
and expenses initially payable to the
Credit Provider for any such credit
enhancement or liquidity support
may be paid from the proceeds of the
Bonds to which such credit enhancement or liquidity support applies. The
Supplemental Trust Agreement for
any Series of Bonds to which any such
credit enhancement or liquidity support applies may include provisions
permitting the Credit Provider to act
as, or in the place of, the holders of
such Bonds for the purposes and on
the terms and conditions set forth in
such Supplemental Trust Agreement.
(e) Bond Anticipation Notes. In
anticipation of the issuance of any
Series of Additional Bonds, the City
may issue one or more Series of Bond
Anticipation Notes. All requirements
of the Trust Agreement applicable to
Bonds shall apply to Bond Anticipation Notes, including, without limitation the conditions precedent for the
issuance of a Series of Bonds. For the
purpose of (i) determining compliance with the rate covenant set forth
in Section 20(c) of this General Bond
Ordinance for any period prior to the
date of calculation, (ii) determining
whether Additional Bonds may be
issued in compliance with the requirements in subsection (h)(iii) of this
Section when any Bond Anticipation
Notes are outstanding, (iii) determining whether Bond Anticipation Notes
may be issued in compliance with the
requirements in subsection (h)(iii) of
this Section, and (iv) determining the
amount of the Debt Service Reserve
Requirement attributable to such
Bond Anticipation Notes, the Debt
Service payable on any Bond Anticipation Notes shall be computed for
purposes of the Trust Agreement in
accordance with Section 7(b) hereof.
(f) Debt Service Reserve Requirement.
In
connection
with
any
issuance of Bonds, the City may, in
the applicable Supplemental Trust
Agreement, provide that no deposit to
the Debt Service Reserve Fund shall
be made for or with respect to such
Additional Bonds, in which case: (i)
the holders of such Additional Bonds
shall have no right or entitlement to
have any portion of the Bond Service
Charges on such Additional Bonds be
paid from any amounts in the Debt
Service Reserve Fund, (ii) the lien of
and pledge on the Debt Service
Reserve Fund shall not extend to or
be for the benefit of the holders of
such Bonds, and (iii) the Debt Service
on such Bonds shall not be taken into

161

51
account in determining the Debt Service Reserve Requirement.
In the event that the Supplemental
Trust Agreement applicable to an
issue of Additional Bonds provides as
described in the preceding paragraph,
then such Supplemental Trust Agreement may also provide for the creation of a special reserve account
solely for such Bonds, separate from
the Debt Service Reserve Fund, and
may provide for the deposit therein,
at the time of issuance or in one or
more subsequent deposits thereto, of
an amount specified in the applicable
Supplemental Trust Agreement as the
required reserve for such Bonds, or
may require the City to provide a
municipal bond insurance policy, a
bank letter or line of credit, or any
other form of credit or liquidity facility issued by a Qualified Financial
Institution to enhance the security for
such Bonds in lieu of a funded reserve
account. If the Supplemental Trust
Agreement applicable to such a Series
of Bonds so provides for such a special reserve account and further
requires that deposits be made thereto from Net Revenues at any time,
then such deposits may be made only
from moneys remaining in the Revenue Fund on the last day of a month
after any required deposits to the
Debt Service Reserve Fund.
If the Supplemental Trust Agreement applicable to a Series of Bonds
provides for no reserve account, or for
a special reserve account as permitted by the preceding paragraph, then
such Supplemental Trust Agreement
shall also provide that the amount of
any defaulted principal of or interest
on such Series of Bonds that would
have been timely paid had the Debt
Service Reserve Requirement for
such Bonds been funded in the Debt
Service Reserve Fund shall be paid
only from moneys remaining in the
Revenue Fund on the last day of a
month after any required deposits to
the Debt Service Reserve Fund.

The Supplemental Bond Ordinance
for any Series of Bonds may provide
that the rate or rates of interest to be

Series Certificate of Award, subject to

Section 6. Subordinated Indebtedness.
(a) The City may, at any time and
from time to time, issue or incur Subordinated Indebtedness for the purpose of financing any Capital Costs,
provided that such Subordinated
Indebtedness is secured solely by, and
is payable solely from, moneys on
deposit in the Subordinated Debt Service Fund, or the Balance Subfund or
both.
(b) Any Supplemental Trust Agreement providing for the issuance of
Subordinated Indebtedness shall provide that the trustee for such Subordinated Indebtedness shall have no
right, power or authority to cause
acceleration of such Subordinated
Indebtedness unless and until the
Trustee has exercised its power to
accelerate the Bonds.
Section 7. Computation of Debt Service.
(a) In the event that all or any portion of any Series of Bonds have been
issued as or are proposed to be issued
as Variable Rate Bonds, then, except
as otherwise provided in paragraph
(f) of this Section, in order to compute
the Debt Service on such Bonds for
the purposes of the Trust Agreement,
the following rules shall apply:
(i) For the purpose of determining
compliance with the rate covenant set
forth in Section 20(c) of this General
Bond Ordinance for any period prior
to the date of calculation, the rate of
interest borne by any Outstanding
Variable Rate Bonds shall be deemed
to be the actual weighted average
rate in effect thereon during such
period;
(ii) For the purpose of determining
whether Bonds may be issued in compliance with the requirements in subsection (h)(iii) of Section 5 of this
General Bond Ordinance, regardless
of whether such Bonds are to be Variable Rate Bonds, the rate of interest
to be borne by any Outstanding Variable Rate Bonds shall be deemed to be
the highest rate of interest borne by
such Variable Rate Bonds during the
preceding twenty-four (24) months,
but if such Variable Rate Bonds have
not been outstanding for twenty-four
(24) months preceding the date of the
computation, then it is to be assumed
that such Variable Rate Bonds will

162

February 3, 2016
bear interest at a fixed interest rate
equal to 120% of the highest rate
applicable within the twenty-four
(24) months immediately preceding
the date of the computation under an
index generally accepted in the securities industry for securities having
ratings and maturity or tender dates
comparable to those of the Outstanding Variable Rate Bonds.
(iii) For the purpose of determining
whether Bonds that are to be Variable
Rate Bonds may be issued in compliance with the requirements in subsection (h)(iii) of Section 5 of this General Bond Ordinance, and for the purpose of determining the amount of the
Debt Service Reserve Requirement, if
any, attributable to such Variable
Rate Bonds, the rate of interest to be
borne by such Variable Rate Bonds
shall be deemed to be a fixed interest
rate equal to 120% of the highest rate
applicable within the twenty-four
(24) months immediately preceding
the date of the computation under an
index generally accepted in the securities industry for securities having
ratings and maturity or tender dates
comparable to those of the proposed
Variable Rate Bonds.
(iv) For the purpose of determining
whether any Outstanding Variable
Rate Bond is deemed paid and discharged for purposes of Article VIII
of the Master Trust Agreement, such
Variable Rate Bond shall be deemed
to bear interest at the actual rate of
interest borne thereby for the remainder of the period that such rate shall
remain in effect, and for any subsequent period prior to the date on
which such Variable Rate Bond is
actually to be paid and discharged,
such Variable Rate Bond shall be
deemed to bear interest at the maximum rate of interest such Variable
Rate Bond may bear pursuant to the
Supplemental
Trust
Agreement
applicable thereto.
(b) Regarding any Bonds that are
or are proposed to be issued as Balloon Bonds, for the purpose of (i)
determining compliance with the rate
covenant set forth in subsection (c) of
Section 20 of this General Bond Ordinance for any period prior to the date
of calculation, (ii) determining
whether Bonds, regardless of whether
they are to be Balloon Bonds, may be
issued in compliance with the requirements in subsection (h)(iii) of Section 5 of this General Bond Ordinance
when any Balloon Bonds are outstanding, (iii) determining whether
Bonds that are to be Balloon Bonds
may be issued in compliance with the
requirements in subsection (h)(iii) of
Section 5 of this General Bond Ordinance, and (iv) determining the
amount of the Debt Service Reserve
Requirement, if any, attributable to
such Balloon Bonds, the Debt Service
on such Bonds shall be determined:
(A) if such Balloon Bonds are not
Capital
Appreciation
Bonds,
by
assuming that such Balloon Bonds
are to be amortized on the basis of
level debt service over the Assumed
Amortization Period and that such
Bonds bear interest at the Assumed
Interest Rate; and
(B) if such Balloon Bonds are Capital Appreciation Bonds, by assuming
that
the
Appreciated
Principal
Amount of such Bonds at maturity is
to be amortized on the basis of level
principal payments over the Assumed
Amortization Period.
(c) If any outstanding Bonds have
been refunded by any Crossover

February 3, 2016
Refunding Bonds, then any principal
of and premium on such Crossover
Refunded Bonds to be paid from a
Crossover Escrow Fund shall be
excluded from Debt Service. If any
outstanding Bonds are Crossover
Refunding Bonds issued to refund
any Bonds, then any interest paid or
to be paid on such Crossover Refunding Bonds from any Crossover
Escrow Fund shall be excluded from
Debt Service.
(d) Debt Service shall not include
payments potentially required to be
made by the City under any Reimbursement Agreement to reimburse
any Credit Provider for payments
made to pay the principal of or interest or any premium on the Bonds, but
Debt Service shall include such payments if the City’s obligation to make
such payments shall have accrued
and become actual.
(e) Regarding any Bonds that are
or are proposed to be issued as Capital
Appreciation Bonds, for the purpose
of (i) determining compliance with
the rate covenant set forth in subsection (c) of Section 20 of this General
Bond Ordinance for any period prior
to the date of calculation, (ii) determining whether Bonds, regardless of
whether they are to be Capital Appreciation Bonds, may be issued in compliance with the requirements in subsection (h)(iii) of Section 5 of this
General Bond Ordinance when any
Capital Appreciation Bonds are outstanding, (iii) determining whether
Bonds that are to be Capital Appreciation Bonds may be issued in compliance with the requirements in subsection (h)(iii) of Section 5 of this General Bond Ordinance, and (iv) determining the amount of the Debt Service Reserve Requirement attributable to such Capital Appreciation
Bonds, the Debt Service on such
Bonds shall include the Appreciated
Principal Amounts at maturity.
(f) If the City enters into an Interest Rate Hedge Agreement to simulate a fixed rate of interest on Variable Rate Bonds, then the City may
(1) secure the portion of the payment
obligations of the City thereunder
that represents the equivalent of
interest on the notional amount of the
Interest Rate Hedge Agreement with
a pledge of the Net Revenues on a parity with the pledge thereof that
secures the Bonds, and (2) cause the
debt structure that is simulated
through the combination of the Variable Rate Bonds with such Interest
Rate Hedge Agreement to apply for
purposes of calculating or projecting
the Debt Service on such Variable
Rate Bonds for any period of time during which such Interest Rate Hedge
Agreement is to be effective, provided
that (i) the debt structure that is simulated through the combination of the
Variable Rate Bonds with such Interest Rate Hedge Agreement complies
with the restrictions of the Trust
Agreement on the terms of and security for the Bonds applied to that
structure as though it consisted
entirely of Bonds and as though the
portion of the payment obligations of
the City thereunder that represents
the equivalent of interest on the
notional amount of the Interest Rate
Hedge Agreement payable to the
counterparty to the Interest Rate
Hedge Agreement constituted Bond
Service Charges, (ii) the counterparty to any swap agreement and the
provider of any interest rate cap is
rated either of the two highest rating

The City Record
categories by at least two Rating
Agencies, (iii) no such Interest Rate
Hedge Agreement purports to entitle
the counterparty to the Interest Rate
Hedge Agreement to payment by the
City from any source other than the
Net Revenues, but such Interest Rate
Hedge Agreement may provide for
securing any portion of the payment
obligations of the City thereunder
that represents the equivalent of
interest on the notional amount of the
Interest Rate Hedge Agreement (but
does not represent, among other
things, any termination payment that
may be payable by the City thereunder) with a pledge of the Net Revenues on a parity with the pledge
thereof that secures the Bonds; and
(iv) the cost of obtaining such Interest Rate Hedge Agreement has been
determined
by
the
Director
of
Finance (who may obtain the written
advice of a Financial Advisor) to be
justified by the corresponding benefit
to the City and to be commercially
reasonable based on then current
market conditions. In the event the
City enters into any such Interest
Rate Hedge Agreement, it shall not
exercise any option to terminate such
Interest Rate Hedge Agreement
unless the Variable Rate Bonds to
which such Interest Rate Hedge
Agreement had related and that will
remain outstanding after the termination thereof would fulfill the requirements of the Trust Agreement as they
apply to Variable Rate Bonds, as
though such Variable Rate Bonds
were being issued on the date of the
termination of such Interest Rate
Hedge Agreement. If deposits to the
Debt Service Fund for Parity Swap
Obligations created pursuant this
paragraph are required to be made
more frequently than had been
required for Bond Service Charges on
any Outstanding Bonds, then, from
and after the time such deposits for
Parity Swap Obligations commence,
deposits to the Debt Service Fund
shall be required for all Outstanding
Bonds with the same frequency as
they are required for such Parity
Swap Obligations.
(g) If the City enters into an Interest Rate Hedge Agreement to simulate a variable rate of interest on
fixed rate Bonds, then the City may
(1) secure the portion of the payment
obligations of the City thereunder
that represents the equivalent of
interest on the notional amount of the
Interest Rate Hedge Agreement with
a pledge of the Net Revenues on a parity with the pledge thereof that
secures the Bonds, and (2) cause the
debt structure that is simulated
through the combination of the fixed
rate Bonds with such Interest Rate
Hedge Agreement to apply for purposes of calculating or projecting the
Debt Service on such fixed rate Bonds
for any period of time during which
such Interest Rate Hedge Agreement
is to be effective, provided that (i) the
debt structure that is simulated
through the combination of the fixed
rate Bonds with such Interest Rate
Hedge Agreement complies with the
restrictions of the Trust Agreement
on the terms of and security for the

Outstanding Bonds with the same frequency as they are required for such
Parity Swap Obligations.
Section 8. Establishment of Funds
and Subfunds.
(a) The City hereby establishes and
creates the following special trust
funds and subfunds:
(1) Construction Fund;
(2) Revenue Fund, containing:
an Operating Subfund, a Working
Capital Subfund, and a
Balance Subfund;
(3) Debt Service Fund, containing
an
Interest Subfund, and
Principal Subfund;
(4) Debt Service Reserve Fund;
(5) Subordinated Debt Service
Fund;
(6) Contingency Fund;
(7) Rate Stabilization Fund; and
(8) Rebate Fund.
(b) The Trustee shall establish (i)
separate subaccounts in the Interest
Subfund and Principal Subfund of the
Debt Service Fund for each Series of
Bonds, (ii) separate subaccounts in
the Debt Service Reserve Fund for
any and each Series of Bonds to which
the Debt Service Reserve Fund
applies, and (iii) separate subaccounts in the Construction Fund for

54
each Series of Bonds with proceeds
required to be deposited in the Construction Fund.
(c) The Revenue Fund and the Subfunds therein, the Contingency Fund
and the Rate Stabilization Fund each
shall be held by the City and not commingled with other moneys of the
City except for purposes of investment. The Debt Service Fund, Debt
Service Reserve Fund, Construction
Fund and Rebate Fund each shall be
held by the Trustee. The Subordinated Debt Service Fund shall be held by
the City or by the Trustee or such
trustee or other party as may be specified in the trust agreement or other
contract between the City and the
holder or holders of the Subordinated
Indebtedness. All moneys or securities deposited with the Trustee pursuant to the Trust Agreement shall be
held in trust and applied only in
accordance with the provisions hereof
and shall be considered trust funds
for the purposes of the Trust Agreement.
Section 9. Construction Fund.
(a) There shall be deposited from
time to time in the Construction Fund
the portion of the proceeds of the
Bonds required to be deposited therein by any Supplemental Bond Ordinance and Supplemental Trust Agreement.
(b) Amounts in the Construction
Fund shall be expended only to pay
Capital Costs and Costs of Issuance or
to cure any deficiency in the Debt Service Fund or the Debt Service Reserve
Fund following the deposits required
pursuant to Section 10 hereof.
Section 10. Revenue Fund. From
and after the authentication and
delivery of the Series 2016 Bonds to
the Original Purchasers thereof, the
City shall cause all cash receipts that
constitute Revenues and any amounts
that the City elects to transfer to the
Revenue Fund from the Rate Stabilization Fund pursuant to Section 15
to be deposited promptly in the Revenue Fund. In each month, the
amounts in the Revenue Fund shall
be deposited in the Operating Subfund and first applied to the payment
of Operating Expenses; thereafter,
the balance in the Revenue Fund up
to the Working Capital Reserve shall
be deposited in the Working Capital
Reserve Subfund and retained as a
reserve for the payment of Operating
Expenses and used for that purpose if
the Operating Subfund shall have
been fully expended; and thereafter,
the balance in the Revenue Fund
shall be paid at the times and in the
amounts as follows:
(a) To the Trustee for deposit in the
Debt Service Fund as follows:
1. Monthly, on or before the last day
of each month, the City shall pay to
the Trustee, for deposit in each subaccount in the Interest Subfund in the
Debt Service Fund, an amount equal
to one-sixth of the amount of interest
due on the next Interest Payment
Date on the Outstanding Bonds of the
Series to which such subaccount
relates; provided, however, that if
fewer than six months precede the
next Interest Payment Date, then, on
or before the last day of each such
month an amount that, if deposited in
each such month, would equal the
amount of interest due on the next
Interest Payment Date on the Outstanding Bonds of the Series to which
such subaccount relates shall be
deposited therein; provided further,
however, such monthly payments

The City Record
need be made only to the extent that
the amount then on deposit in any
such subaccount is less than the
amount required to be on deposit
therein in accordance herewith; and
provided yet further, however, that
the frequency and amount of any
deposits required by this paragraph
shall be subject to adjustment pursuant to Sections 5(b) or 7(f) or (g) of
this General Bond Ordinance.
2. Monthly, on or before the last day
of each of the twelve months that precede a month in which a Serial Maturity Date occurs or a Sinking Fund
Installment is due, the City shall pay
to the Trustee for deposit in each
applicable subaccount in the Principal Subfund in the Debt Service Fund
an amount equal to one-twelfth of the
amount necessary to provide for the
payment of the principal due on the
next Serial Maturity Date or of the
next Sinking Fund Installment; provided, however, that if fewer than
twelve months precede the next
month in which a Serial Maturity
Date occurs or a Sinking Fund Installment is due, then, on or before the last
day of each such month an amount
that, if deposited in each such month,
would equal the amount of principal
due on the next Serial Maturity Date
or of the next Sinking Fund Installment for the Outstanding Bonds of the
Series to which such subaccount
relates shall be deposited therein; provided further, however, such monthly
payments need be made only to the
extent that the amount then on
deposit in any such subaccount is less
than the amount required to be on
deposit therein in accordance herewith; and provided yet further, however, that the frequency and amount
of any deposits required by this paragraph shall be subject to adjustment
pursuant to Sections 5(b) or 7(f) or
(g) of this General Bond Ordinance.
(b) To the Trustee for deposit in the
Debt Service Reserve Fund, monthly
on or before the last day of each
month, commencing on the date set
forth in the applicable Supplemental
Bond Ordinance with respect to any
Series of Bonds for which the Debt
Service Reserve Requirement is to be
deposited in the Debt Service Reserve

established in the Debt Service
Reserve Fund for such Series of Additional Bonds, an amount such that, if
that same amount were deposited in
equal monthly installments, the

to the Debt Service Reserve Requirement with respect to such Series of
Additional Bonds on the fifth (5th)
anniversary of such commencement
date, after giving effect to any
amounts already on deposit therein
and pledged to such Series of Additional Bonds. Thereafter, if the
amount on deposit in such subaccount
at any time is less than the Debt Service Reserve Requirement with
respect to such Series of Additional
Bonds, the City shall pay to the
Trustee for deposit in such subaccount, on the before following the
date of such deficiency, an amount
equal to one-twelfth of such deficiency. The frequency and amount of any
deposits required by this paragraph
shall be subject to adjustment pursuant to Sections 5(b) or 7(f) or (g)
and 10(a) of this General Bond Ordinance so that the deposits required by
this paragraph for any Series of

Section 11. Debt Service Fund.
(a) The Trustee shall pay out of the
applicable subaccounts in the Interest Subfund and in the Principal Subfund in the applicable Debt Service
Fund to each Paying Agent (i) on or
before each Interest Payment Date
for the Bonds of each Series (x) the
amount required for the interest
payable on all such Outstanding
Bonds on such date and (y) the
amount, if any, required for the payment of the principal maturing on all
such Outstanding Bonds on such date,
as provided in Section 10(a)(2) hereof, and (ii) on or before the day preceding the redemption date for any
such Bonds to be redeemed at the
option of the City, the amount
required for the payment of such
Bonds then to be redeemed. Such
amounts shall be so applied by each
Paying Agent on and after the due
date thereof.

February 3, 2016
(b) The City shall pay to the
Trustee for deposit in the Debt Service Fund any moneys held in any
other Funds or Subfunds in excess of
the amounts required to be maintained therein that the City has elected to apply to the redemption prior to
maturity of any Bonds, and such
amounts shall be so applied by the
Trustee in the manner and at the
times provided in the Trust Agreement.
(c) Amounts in the applicable subaccount in the Principal Subfund for
the payment of any Sinking Fund
Installment for the Term Bonds of
any Series then Outstanding (together with amounts in the applicable subaccount in the Interest Subfund with
respect to the Term Bonds for which
such Sinking Fund Installment was
established) shall be applied by the
Trustee to the redemption of Term
Bonds of the Series and maturity for
which such Sinking Fund Installment
was established in an amount not
exceeding that necessary to effect the
mandatory redemption of such Term
Bonds on the Mandatory Redemption
Dates. The Trustee shall, by giving
notice as provided in the Trust Agreement, proceed to call for redemption
on the due date of any such Sinking
Fund Installment the Term Bonds of
the Series and maturity for which
such Sinking Fund Installment was
established (except in the case of
Term Bonds maturing on a Sinking
Fund Installment date), in such
amount as shall be necessary to effect
the mandatory redemption of such
Term Bonds on the Mandatory
Redemption Date in an amount equal
to the amount of such Sinking Fund
Installment. The principal amount of
Term Bonds of such Series and maturity theretofore delivered by the City
to the Trustee to satisfy such Sinking
Fund Installment, in the manner and
to the extent as may be provided in
this General Bond Ordinance or in the
Supplemental Bond Ordinance or Supplemental Trust Agreement authorizing such Series, shall be credited
against the amount of such Sinking
Fund Installment. Such notice shall
be given regardless of whether or not
moneys therefor shall have been
deposited in the Principal Subfund in
the applicable Debt Service Fund and
without any instructions of the City.
The Trustee shall pay out of the Principal Subfund in the applicable Debt
Service Fund to the appropriate Paying Agent, on or before the day preceding such Mandatory Redemption
Date, the amount required for the
redemption of the Term Bonds so
called for redemption, and such
amount shall be applied by such Paying Agent to such redemption. All
expenses in connection with such
redemption of Term Bonds shall be
paid by the City from the Operating
Subfund.
(d) To the extent that a Series of
Bonds is secured by credit enhancement or liquidity support provided by
a Credit Provider pursuant to a Reimbursement Agreement, the Supplemental Bond Ordinance and Supplemental Trust Agreement with respect
to that Series may provide that the
Trustee shall apply amounts in the
Debt Service Fund first, to the payment of Bond Service Charges and
any Parity Swap Obligations then due
and, second, to the payment of any
Credit Obligations then due.

Section 12. Debt Service Reserve
Fund.
If on any Interest Payment Date,
the amount in the subaccount in the
Interest Subfund or the Principal Subfund for any Series of Bonds shall be
less than the amount required to be
therein on deposit pursuant to Section
10 hereof, the Trustee shall, after
deposits are made, if any, pursuant to
Sections 13, 14, 15 and 16 hereof, apply
the amounts in the applicable Subfund, if any, in the Debt Service
Reserve Fund to the extent necessary
to make good any such deficiency (or
the entire amount in the applicable
Subfund if less than sufficient). The
City may, so long as it will not result
in a reduction of the rating assigned
to any of the Bonds, substitute for
funds on deposit in the Debt Service
Reserve Fund a letter of credit, surety
bond or other credit enhancement
facility issued by a Qualified Financial Institution.
Section 13. Subordinated Debt Service Fund.
(a) If on the third (3rd) day before
any Interest Payment Date, the
amount in any of the Subfunds in the
Debt Service Fund shall be less than
the amount required to be on deposit
therein pursuant to Section 10 hereof,
after deposits, if any, are made pursuant to Sections 14, 15 and 16 hereof,
the City shall, upon the request of the
Trustee, transfer or cause the transfer of moneys from the Subordinated
Debt Service Fund to the Trustee to
make good any such deficiency (or
the entire amount in the Subordinated
Debt Service Fund if less than sufficient).
(b) If on any day next following the
date of a payment and deposit
required by Section 10(b) hereof, the
amount in any of the Subfunds in the
Debt Service Reserve Fund shall be
less than the amount required to be on
deposit therein pursuant to Section
10(b), the City shall, upon the request
of the Trustee, transfer moneys from
the Subordinated Debt Service Fund
to the Trustee for deposit in the
appropriate Subfund in the Debt Service Reserve Fund an amount sufficient to cure any such deficiency (or
the entire amount in the Subordinated
Debt Service Fund if less than sufficient).
(c) Subject to the provisions of subsections (a) and (b) above and Section 17, the amounts on deposit in the
Subordinated Debt Service Fund shall
be applied to the payment of the principal of and interest and any premium
on Subordinated Indebtedness as and
when due or to the required funding
of any special reserve account established for any Subordinated Indebtedness.
Consistent with Section 10(c), if
any Supplemental Trust Agreement
or other contract between the City
and the holder or holders of Subordinated Indebtedness requires the
establishment and funding of a
reserve account related to such Subordinated Indebtedness, then any moneys in any such reserve account shall
be required to be transferred pursuant to subsections (a) and (b)
above prior to the transfer of moneys
from the Subordinated Debt Service
Fund for the purposes stated in those
subsections. Subject to the required
uses under subsections (a) and (b)
above, amounts on deposit in any
such reserve account shall be transferred to the Subordinated Debt Service Fund to cure any deficiency in

165

55
the Subordinated Debt Service Fund
on any date on which the payment of
the principal of or interest or any premium on Subordinated Indebtedness
is due.
Section 14. Contingency Fund.
(a) If on the third (3rd) day before
any Interest Payment Date, the
amount in any of the Subfunds in the
Debt Service Fund shall be less than
the amount required to be on deposit
therein pursuant to Section 10 hereof,
after deposits, if any, are made pursuant to Sections 15 and 16 hereof, the
City shall, upon the request of the
Trustee, transfer or cause the transfer of moneys from the Contingency
Fund to the Trustee to the extent necessary to make good any such deficiency (or the entire amount in the
Contingency Fund if less than sufficient).
(b) If on any day next following the
date of a payment and deposit
required by Section 10(b) hereof, the
amount in any of the Subfunds in the
Debt Service Reserve Fund shall be
less than the amount required to be on
deposit therein pursuant to Section
10(b), the City shall, upon the request
of the Trustee, transfer moneys from
the Contingency Fund to the Trustee
for deposit in the appropriate Subfund
in the Debt Service Reserve Fund an
amount sufficient to cure any such
deficiency (or the entire amount in
the Contingency Fund if less than sufficient).
(c) Subject to the provisions of subsections (a) and (b) above and Section 17, the amounts on deposit in the
Contingency Fund shall be used only
for the payment of Capital Costs or
for the purpose of redeeming Bonds.
Section 15. Rate Stabilization Fund.
(a) If on the third (3rd) day before
any Interest Payment Date, the
amount in any of the Subfunds in the
Debt Service Fund shall be less than
the amount required to be on deposit
therein pursuant to Section 10 hereof,
after deposits, if any, are made pursuant to Section 16 hereof, the City
shall, upon the request of the Trustee,
transfer or cause the transfer of moneys from the Rate Stabilization Fund
to the Trustee to make good any such
deficiency (or the entire amount in
the Rate Stabilization Fund if less
than sufficient).
(b) If on any day next following the
date of a payment and deposit
required by Section 10(b) hereof, the
amount in any of the Subfunds in the
Debt Service Reserve Fund shall be
less than the amount required to be on
deposit therein pursuant to Section
10(b), the City shall, upon the request
of the Trustee, transfer moneys from
the Rate Stabilization Fund to the
Trustee for deposit in the appropriate
Subfund in the Debt Service Reserve
Fund an amount sufficient to cure
any such deficiency (or the entire
amount in the Rate Stabilization
Fund if less than sufficient).
(c) Subject to the provisions of subsections (a) and (b) above and Section 17, the City may from time to time
transfer amounts on deposit in the
Rate Stabilization Fund to the Revenue Fund and cause them to be
applied as Revenues pursuant to Section 10.
Section 16. Balance Subfund.
(a) If on the third (3rd) day before
any Interest Payment Date, the

Debt Service Fund shall be less than
the amount required to be on deposit
therein pursuant to Section 10 hereof,

the City shall, upon the request of the

Section 17. Rebate Fund. There is
hereby established and ordered to be
maintained as a separate deposit
account (except when invested as
hereinafter provided) in the custody
of the Trustee a Rebate Fund. Any
provision hereof or of the Trust
Agreement to the contrary notwithstanding, the Rebate Fund is not
pledged to the payment of Bond Service Charges, is not one of or part of
any of the Special Funds, and is free
and clear of any lien hereunder. Separate accounts shall be created in the
Rebate Fund for each Series of Bonds,
commencing with the Series 2016
Bonds.
At least five days prior to the end of
the fifth Bond Year and each fifth
Bond Year thereafter for each Series
of Bonds, including the Series 2016
Bonds, and within five (5) days after
the date on which all outstanding
Bonds of such Series are paid or
deemed paid in full, the City shall calculate or shall furnish information to
and engage an independent certified
public accounting firm that is not
unacceptable to the Trustee, to calculate, the Rebate Amount as of the end
of that Bond Year or the date of such
final payment. The Trustee may rely
upon the City for the calculation of
the Rebate Amount, provided that the
Trustee receives a verification of the
accuracy of such computations by a
firm of independent certified public
accountants or an opinion of nationally recognized bond counsel that such
computations are in compliance with
the Code. Within thirty (30) days
after the end of the fifth (5th) Bond
Year and every fifth (5th) Bond Year
thereafter, the Trustee, acting on
behalf of the City and at the written
direction of the City, shall pay to the
United States in accordance with Section 148(f) of the Code from the moneys then on deposit in the applicable
account in the Rebate Fund an
amount equal to 90% (or such greater

The City Record
percentage not in excess of 100% as
the City may direct the Trustee in
writing to pay) of the Rebate Amount
determined from the date of the original delivery of the Bonds of that
Series (less the portion of the Rebate
Amount, if any, previously paid to the
United States pursuant to this Section). Within sixty (60) days after the
payment in full of all outstanding
Bonds of such Series and upon written
direction of the City, the Trustee shall
pay to the United States in accordance
with Section 148(f) of the Code from
the moneys then on deposit in the
applicable account in the Rebate
Fund an amount equal to 100% of the
Rebate Amount determined from the
date of the original delivery of the
Bonds of that Series to the date of
such payment (but less that portion of
the Rebate Amount, if any, previously
paid to the United States pursuant to
this Section) and any moneys remaining in the applicable account in the
Rebate Fund following such payment
shall be paid to the City. Notwithstanding anything in this General
Bond Ordinance to the contrary, the
moneys needed for any payment
required by the preceding two sentences may be derived from balances
in any of the Special Funds other than
the Debt Service Fund and the Debt
Service Reserve Fund, and the City
agrees to apply those balances to that
purpose in the following Order: the
Balance Subfund, the Rate Stabilization Fund, the Contingency Fund, the
Subordinated Indebtedness Fund and
any related reserve fund or account,
and the Construction Fund.
The Trustee shall keep such
records as are provided to it of the
computations made pursuant to this
Section as are required under Section
148(f) of the Code.
The Trustee shall keep and make
available to the City such records concerning the investments of the gross
proceeds of the Bonds and the investments of earnings from those investments as may be requested by the
City in order to enable the City to
make the computations required
under Section 148(f) of the Code.
If all the gross proceeds of the
Bonds of any Series, within the meaning of Section 148(f) of the Code, are
expended for the governmental purpose for which that Series of Bonds
was issued within six (6) months of
the date of issuance of that Series and
it is not expected that any other gross
proceeds of that Series of Bonds will
arise in the future, the provisions of
this Section 17 apply only to gross proceeds of that Series of Bonds, if any,
that actually do subsequently arise.
At the written request of the City,
any moneys held as part of the Rebate
Fund shall be invested or reinvested
by the Trustee in Eligible Investments. At no time shall any funds constituting gross proceeds of any such
Series of Bonds be used in any manner
to cause or result in a prohibited payment under applicable Treasury Regulations pertaining to, or in any other
fashion as would constitute failure of
compliance with, Section 148 of the
Code.
If at any time the City has received
a written opinion of Bond Counsel
that failure to comply with this Section 17 or any part hereof would not
adversely affect the exclusion of
interest on any Tax-Exempt Bonds
from gross income for federal income
tax purposes, the City may discontinue compliance with this Section 17 to
the extent set forth in such opinion.
